}\n}\n\nimpl SpecificCSSRule for CSSContainerRule {\n    fn ty(&self) -> CssRuleType {\n        CssRuleType::Container\n    }\n\n    fn get_css(&self) -> DOMString {\n        let guard = This enables the CSSOM API to expose parsed `@container` rules to JavaScript code, allowing web applications and tests to access and manipulate container query rules.\n\n## Implementation Details\n\n### 1. Core DOM Implementation\n**File: `components/script/dom/css/csscontainerrule.rs`**\n- Implements `CSSContainerRule` struct as a DOM wrapper\n- Inherits from `CSSConditionRule` to leverage grouping rule functionality\n- Wraps stylo's `Arc<ContainerRule>` type\n- Implements `SpecificCSSRule` trait for integration with CSS cascade\n- Implements `CSSContainerRuleMethods` WebIDL binding\n- Provides `get_condition_text()` method for accessing rule conditions (e.g., \"(min-width: 100px)\")\n\n**Key Methods:**\n- `new()` - Creates a new CSSContainerRule with DOM reflection\n- `get_condition_text()` - Returns the container query condition as a string\n- `update_rule()` - Updates rule when stylesheets change\n\n### 2. WebIDL Binding\n**File: `components/script_bindings/webidls/CSSContainerRule.webidl`**\n- Defines the JavaScript-accessible interface for `CSSContainerRule`\n- Inherits from `CSSConditionRule` to provide grouping rule methods\n- Automatically generates DOM binding code via WebIDL generator\n\n### 3. CSS Module Integration\n**File: `components/script/dom/css/mod.rs` (Updated)**\n- Registered `csscontainerrule` module\n- Enables module compilation and visibility\n\n### 4. CSS Rule Dispatcher\n**File: `components/script/dom/css/cssrule.rs` (Updated)**\n- Added `CSSContainerRule` to type union in `as_specific()` method\n- Added pattern matching for `StyleCssRule::Container` in `new_specific()`\n- Added pattern matching for `StyleCssRule::Container` in `update_rule()`\n\n**These changes ensure:**\n- Container rules are properly cast when accessed via CSSOM\n- Container rules are instantiated as CSSContainerRule objects\n- Rule updates propagate correctly through the DOM\n\n### 5. Condition Rule Integration\n**File: `components/script/dom/css/cssconditionrule.rs` (Updated)**\n- Added `CSSContainerRule` handling in `ConditionText()` method\n- Enables JavaScript access to container query conditions\n- Example: `rule.conditionText` returns `\"(min-width: 100px)\"`\n\n## Architecture\n\n```\n┌─────────────────────────────────────────┐\n│  CSS Parser (Stylo/External)            │\n│  Parses @container rules                │\n└──────────────────┬──────────────────────┘\n                   │\n                   ▼ Creates StyleCssRule::Container\n┌─────────────────────────────────────────┐\n│  CSSRule::new_specific() (Dispatcher)    │\n│  Matches on Container variant           │\n└──────────────────┬──────────────────────┘\n                   │\n                   ▼ Creates DomRoot<CSSContainerRule>\n┌─────────────────────────────────────────┐\n│  CSSContainerRule (DOM Wrapper)          │\n│  - Queryable via `rule.conditionText` property\n✅ **Rule Serialization** - Rules serialize back to CSS text\n✅ **Cascade Integration** - Works with CSS cascade through grouping rule interface\n\n## Test Compatibility\n\nThe implementation supports:\n- IDL interface tests (`idlharness.html`)\n- CSSOM rule access tests\n- Nested container query tests\n- Rule serialization tests\n- Style application through @container rules\n\nExample test case that now works:\n```javascript\nconst rule = document.styleSheets[0].cssRules[0];\nconsole.log(rule instanceof CSSContainerRule); // true\nconsole.log(rule.conditionText); // \"(min-width: 100px)\"\nconsole.log(rule.cssRules[0]); // Access nested rules\n```\n\n## Integration Points\n\n1. **Parser** → Creates `StyleCssRule::Container` (handled by stylo)\n2. **Rule Dispatcher** → Converts to `CSSContainerRule` (implemented ✓)\n3. **CSSOM API** → Exposes to JavaScript (WebIDL binding implemented ✓)\n4. **Condition Access** → `conditionText` property (implemented ✓)\n5. **Cascade** → Works through `CSSGroupingRule` (inherited ✓)\n\n## Files Summary\n\n| File | Status | Changes |\n|------|--------|---------|\n| `csscontainerrule.rs` | ✅ Created | New file -
